 i only knew to fight against the current dragging and pulling me around like a rag doll in a washing machine .

 i studied the shore further down the river and waited patiently in the debilitating cold .

 i waited and waited but there was not a single sound , not a single movement other than the falling snowflakes floating to the earth . 
 my adrenaline began to dissipate , naturally reacting to the feeling that there was no immediate danger , from him at least .

 i needed to know she was okay .
